  24 /**
  25  * @test
  26  * @summary Test implicit String concatenations, multiple shapes.
  27  *
  28  * @compile ImplicitStringConcatShapes.java
  29  * @run main/othervm -Xverify:all ImplicitStringConcatShapes
  30  *
  31  * @compile -XDstringConcat=inline ImplicitStringConcatShapes.java
  32  * @run main/othervm -Xverify:all ImplicitStringConcatShapes
  33  *
  34  * @compile -XDstringConcat=indy ImplicitStringConcatShapes.java
  35  * @run main/othervm ImplicitStringConcatShapes
  36  *
  37  * @compile -XDstringConcat=indyWithConstants ImplicitStringConcatShapes.java
  38  * @run main/othervm -Xverify:all ImplicitStringConcatShapes
  39 */
  40 public class ImplicitStringConcatShapes {
  41     public static void test(String expected, String actual) {
  42         // Fingers crossed: String concat should work.
  43         if (!expected.equals(actual)) {
  44             StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
  45             sb.append("Expected = ");
  46             sb.append(expected);
  47             sb.append(", actual = ");
  48             sb.append(actual);
  49             throw new IllegalStateException(sb.toString());
  50         }
  51     }
  52 
  53     static class MyClass {
  54         private final int i;
  55 
  56         public MyClass(int i) {
  57             this.i = i;
  58         }
  59 
  60         public String toString() {
  61             return new StringBuilder("C(").append(i).append(")").toString();
  62         }
  63     }
  64 
  65     static class MyClassNullToString {
  66         public String toString() {
  67             return null;
  68         }
  69     }
  70 
  71     public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
  72         new ImplicitStringConcatShapes().run();
  73     }
